  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>I am getting a deadlock in SYSTABLE. When I turn on Dderby.locks.deadlockTrace=true, I get a StackOverflowException</p> 
                  <p>Derby version The Apache Software Foundation - Apache Derby - 10.3.2.2</p> 
                  <ul class="alternate" type="square"> 
                   <li>(618335): instance 80220011-0119-f93f-b912-00000000bced<br> on database directory /db/domains/geoff </li> 
                  </ul>

(DATABASE =<br> domains/geoff), (DRDAID = null), Cleanup action starting<br> java.lang.StackOverflowError<br> at org.apache.derby.impl.sql.execute.GenericExecutionFactory.getValueRow(Unknown There are two databases, naturally each has a different connection URL. Let\'s call them Database A and Database B. I read in a configuration file that describes a set of tables in Database A, and then I create those tables, and store some information about them in Database B.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003e1) define tables in Database A\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n2) store some information about tables in Database A in a table in Database B\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n3) alter tables in Database A to add a named foreign key constraint to some of the tabes\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n4) store some more information about tables in A into a table in Database B\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe problem only occurs on step 4, and it only occurs when there are 9 insertions into Database B as part of step (4). But until that session commits, another session cannot login \\nwith the same user name, since the new entry in SYSSCHEMAS \\ncorresponding to the new user\'s schema has not been committed either \\n(it has a write lock on it so it can\'t be read by the second session). \\n\\n Note, even if you don\'t use explicit users, there will still be be an \\nimplicit user, so the same thing applies. \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Dag H. Wanvik\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_12602130_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'04\\/Jun\\/08 00:27\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2008-06-04T00:27:00+0000\'\u003e04\\/Jun\\/08 00:27\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e   - \u003cspan class=\\\"redText subText\\\" title=\\\"Dag H. Wanvik - 04\\/Jun\\/08 00:33\\\"\u003eedited\u003c\\/span\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eThis patch, derby-3678-1, adds a testcase, testDerby3678, to\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nLazyDefaultSchemaCreationTest. This reproduces the infinite recursion\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nseen by this issue, if applied without the rest of the patch, which\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nalso contains a fix.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eDescription of the problem:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eA time-out occurs when a second transaction tries to connect if\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nanother connection creates a schema and populates it with a table\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nwithout committing. See also \u003ca href=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/browse\\/DERBY-48\\\" title=\\\" A connection request that has a default schema that is being created by another transaction will fail to connect\\\" class=\\\"issue-link\\\" data-issue-key=\\\"DERBY-48\\\"\u003e\u003cdel\u003eDERBY-48\u003c\\/del\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eIn the repro test case, after the timeout occurs on the second\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nconnect, the code in Timeout.java tries to construct the diagnostic\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nlock table when tracing is enabled\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n(derby.locks.deadlockTrace=true). The first thing Timeout does when\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\ncontructing an exception (inside buildLockTableString), is to create a\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nnew instance of TableNameInfo, which it uses to map conglomerate ids\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nto names to make the print-out more user friendly.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe constructor of TableNameInfo calls\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nDataDictionary#hashAllTableDescriptorsByTableId, which scans\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nSYS.SYSTABLES in read uncommitted mode. When an entry is found, a\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\ndescriptor for that table is built\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n(SYSTABLESRowFactory#buildDescriptor).\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eAs part of building the descriptor for the table, buildDescriptor\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\ntries to look up thats table\'s schema using the UUID of the schema\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n(found in the row from SYSTABLES describing the table) using\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\ndd.getSchemaDescriptor. This method tries to read SYS.SYSSCHEMAS with\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nrepeatable read mode, which leads to the recursive lock and finally\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nstack overflow for the thread.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eIf the lookup of the table\'s schema is done with read uncommitted\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\ninstead, the recursion will not happen. This seems permissible, since\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nSYS.SYSTABLES is also read in read uncommitted mode from\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nhashAllTableDescriptorsByTableId, which is only ever called from\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nTableNameInfo, which, in turn, is only used for diagnostics, as far as\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nI can tell.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ePatch description:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cul class=\\\"alternate\\\" type=\\\"square\\\"\u003e\\n\\t\u003cli\u003eAdds a new testcase to LazyDefaultSchemaCreationTest\u003c\\/li\u003e\\n\\t\u003cli\u003eMakes hashAllTableDescriptorsByTableId use read uncommitted mode when\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  accessing SYS.SYSSCHEMAS. Unfortunately I had to add many overloads\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  to be able to propagate the isolation mode all the way down. Wanvik - 04\\/Jun\\/08 00:33\\\"\u003eedited\u003c\\/span\u003e                   This patch, derby-3678-1, adds a testcase, testDerby3678, to \\nLazyDefaultSchemaCreationTest. This reproduces the infinite recursion \\nseen by this issue, if applied without the rest of the patch, which \\nalso contains a fix. \\n\\n Description of the problem: \\n\\n A time-out occurs when a second transaction tries to connect if \\nanother connection creates a schema and populates it with a table \\nwithout committing. See also   DERBY-48  . \\n\\n In the repro test case, after the timeout occurs on the second \\nconnect, the code in Timeout.java tries to construct the diagnostic \\nlock table when tracing is enabled \\n(derby.locks.deadlockTrace=true). The first thing Timeout does when \\ncontructing an exception (inside buildLockTableString), is to create a \\nnew instance of TableNameInfo, which it uses to map conglomerate ids \\nto names to make the print-out more user friendly. \\n\\n The constructor of TableNameInfo calls \\nDataDictionary#hashAllTableDescriptorsByTableId, which scans \\nSYS.SYSTABLES in read uncommitted mode. When an entry is found, a \\ndescriptor for that table is built \\n(SYSTABLESRowFactory#buildDescriptor). \\n\\n As part of building the descriptor for the table, buildDescriptor \\ntries to look up thats table\'s schema using the UUID of the schema \\n(found in the row from SYSTABLES describing the table) using \\ndd.getSchemaDescriptor. This method tries to read SYS.SYSSCHEMAS with \\nrepeatable read mode, which leads to the recursive lock and finally \\nstack overflow for the thread. \\n\\n If the lookup of the table\'s schema is done with read uncommitted \\ninstead, the recursion will not happen. This seems permissible, since \\nSYS.SYSTABLES is also read in read uncommitted mode from \\nhashAllTableDescriptorsByTableId, which is only ever called from \\nTableNameInfo, which, in turn, is only used for diagnostics, as far as \\nI can tell. \\n\\n Patch description: \\n\\n \\n\\t Adds a new testcase to LazyDefaultSchemaCreationTest \\n\\t Makes hashAllTableDescriptorsByTableId use read uncommitted mode when \\n  accessing SYS.SYSSCHEMAS. Unfortunately I had to add many overloads \\n  to be able to propagate the isolation mode all the way down. Is \\n  there a better way? \\n \\n\\n\\n Running regressions now.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-12602255\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/DERBY-3678?focusedCommentId=12602255&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-12602255\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"dagw\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_12602255_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=dagw\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"dagw\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Dag H.
